I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
[BUG] ACM rejects import of valid certs
## Service

ACM

## AWS API Action

ImportCertificate

## Expected behavior

Successful import

## Actual behavior

HTTP 400 error

ERROR: An error occurred (ValidationException) when calling the ImportCertificate operation: Invalid certificate: Certificate parsing failed: Invalid certificate PEM format

## Reproduction

```bash
# Generate a self-signed cert
openssl req -x509 -newkey rsa:2048 -keyout /tmp/key.pem -out /tmp/cert.pem \
  -days 365 -nodes -subj "/CN=test.example.com" 2>/dev/null

# This works — direct HTTP with PEM as plain string:
curl -s -X POST http://localhost:8081 \
  -H "X-Amz-Target: CertificateManager.ImportCertificate" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/x-amz-json-1.1" \
  -d "{\"Certificate\":\"$(sed ':a;N;$!ba;s/\n/\\n/g' /tmp/cert.pem)\",\"PrivateKey\":\"$(sed ':a;N;$!ba;s/\n/\\n/g' /tmp/key.pem)\"}"

# This fails — AWS CLI base64-encodes blobs per JSON 1.1 spec:
aws acm import-certificate \
  --endpoint-url http://localhost:8081 \
  --certificate fileb:///tmp/cert.pem \
  --private-key fileb:///tmp/key.pem
```

## Environment

- Floci version / image tag: 1.3.0
- Java SDK version (if applicable): 25
- How you're running Floci: `mvn quarkus:dev`
[BUG] ACM refuses to export an imported cert
## Service

ACM

## AWS API Action

ExportCertificate

## Expected behavior

After importing a user-provided certificate, export certificate should be allowed.

## Actual behavior

operation error ACM: ExportCertificate, https response error StatusCode: 400, RequestID: 4dddfc97-4919-4464-ba80-0a6a90385603, api error ValidationException: Certificate is not PRIVATE type and Export is not ENABLED

## Reproduction

```bash
openssl req -x509 -newkey rsa:2048 -keyout /tmp/key.pem -out /tmp/cert.pem \
  -days 365 -nodes -subj "/CN=test.example.com" 2>/dev/null

aws acm import-certificate \
  --endpoint-url http://localhost:8081 \
  --certificate fileb:///tmp/cert.pem \
  --private-key fileb:///tmp/key.pem
For the export bug:

# Import via direct HTTP (workaround for the import bug)
ARN=$(curl -s -X POST http://localhost:8081 \
  -H "X-Amz-Target: CertificateManager.ImportCertificate" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/x-amz-json-1.1" \
  -d "{\"Certificate\":\"$(sed ':a;N;$!ba;s/\n/\\n/g' /tmp/cert.pem)\",\"PrivateKey\":\"$(sed ':a;N;$!ba;s/\n/\\n/g' /tmp/key.pem)\"}" \
  | jq -r .CertificateArn)

aws acm export-certificate \
  --endpoint-url http://localhost:8081 \
  --certificate-arn "$ARN" \
  --passphrase "test-passphrase"
```

## Environment

- Floci version / image tag: 1.3.0
- Java SDK version (if applicable): 25
- How you're running Floci: `mvn quarkus:dev`

   362	
   363	        Certificate cert = new Certificate();
   364	        cert.setArn(arn);
   365	        cert.setDomainName(extractCommonName(x509Cert));
   366	        cert.setStatus(CertificateStatus.ISSUED);
   367	        cert.setType(CertificateType.IMPORTED);
   368	        cert.setCreatedAt(existingArn == null ? now : null);
   369	        cert.setImportedAt(now);
   370	        cert.setIssuedAt(now);
   371	        cert.setNotBefore(x509Cert.getNotBefore().toInstant());
   372	        cert.setNotAfter(x509Cert.getNotAfter().toInstant());
   373	        cert.setSerial(x509Cert.getSerialNumber().toString());
   374	        cert.setSubject(x509Cert.getSubjectX500Principal().getName());
   375	        cert.setIssuer(x509Cert.getIssuerX500Principal().getName());
   376	        cert.setKeyAlgorithm(keyAlg);
   377	        cert.setSignatureAlgorithm(x509Cert.getSigAlgName());
   378	        cert.setCertificateBody(certificatePem);
   379	        cert.setPrivateKey(privateKeyPem);
   380	        cert.setCertificateChain(chainPem);
   381	        cert.setTags(tags != null ? new HashMap<>(tags) : new HashMap<>());
   382	
   383	        String storageKey = regionKey(region, certId);
   384	        store.put(storageKey, cert);
   385	
   386	        LOG.infov("Imported certificate: {0}", arn);
   387	        return cert;
   388	    }
   389	
   390	    // ============ ExportCertificate ============
   391	
   392	    public Certificate exportCertificate(String certificateArn, String passphraseBase64, String region) {
   393	        Certificate cert = getCertificateByArn(certificateArn, region);
   394	
   395	        if (!cert.canExport()) {
   396	            throw new AwsException("ValidationException",
   397	                "Certificate is not PRIVATE type and Export is not ENABLED", 400);
   398	        }
   399	
   400	        String passphrase;
   401	        try {
   402	            passphrase = new String(Base64.getDecoder().decode(passphraseBase64));
   403	        } catch (Exception e) {
   404	            throw new AwsException("ValidationException", "Invalid passphrase encoding", 400);
   405	        }
   406	
   407	        if (passphrase.length() < 4) {
   408	            throw new AwsException("ValidationException", "Passphrase must be at least 4 characters", 400);
   409	        }
   410	
   411	        // Encrypt the private key
   412	        String encryptedKey = certificateGenerator.encryptPrivateKey(cert.getPrivateKey(), passphrase);
   413	
   414	        // Return certificate with encrypted private key
   415	        Certificate exportCert = new Certificate();
   416	        exportCert.setCertificateBody(cert.getCertificateBody());
   417	        exportCert.setCertificateChain(cert.getCertificateChain());
   418	        exportCert.setPrivateKey(encryptedKey);
   419	        return exportCert;
   420	    }
   421	
   422	    // ============ Tagging Operations ============
   423	
   424	    public void addTagsToCertificate(String certificateArn, Map<String, String> tags, String region) {
   425	        Certificate cert = getCertificateByArn(certificateArn, region);
   426	        validateTags(tags);
   427	
   428	        Map<String, String> currentTags = cert.getTags() != null ? new HashMap<>(cert.getTags()) : new HashMap<>();
   429	        currentTags.putAll(tags);
   430

   180	     * @param privateKeyPem The private key in PEM format
   181	     * @param passphrase The passphrase for encryption
   182	     * @return Encrypted private key in PEM format
   183	     */
   184	    public String encryptPrivateKey(String privateKeyPem, String passphrase) {
   185	        try {
   186	            PrivateKey privateKey = parsePrivateKey(privateKeyPem);
   187	
   188	            // Use AES-256-CBC instead of deprecated Triple-DES
   189	            JcePKCSPBEOutputEncryptorBuilder encryptorBuilder = new JcePKCSPBEOutputEncryptorBuilder(
   190	                NISTObjectIdentifiers.id_aes256_CBC
   191	            );
   192	            encryptorBuilder.setProvider(BouncyCastleProvider.PROVIDER_NAME);
   193	
   194	            PKCS8EncryptedPrivateKeyInfoBuilder pkcs8Builder = new JcaPKCS8EncryptedPrivateKeyInfoBuilder(privateKey);
   195	            PKCS8EncryptedPrivateKeyInfo encryptedInfo = pkcs8Builder.build(
   196	                encryptorBuilder.build(passphrase.toCharArray())
   197	            );
   198	
   199	            StringWriter sw = new StringWriter();
   200	            try (JcaPEMWriter pemWriter = new JcaPEMWriter(sw)) {
   201	                pemWriter.writeObject(encryptedInfo);
   202	            }
   203	            return sw.toString();
   204	
   205	        } catch (Exception e) {
   206	            LOG.error("Failed to encrypt private key", e);
   207	            throw new CertificateGenerationException("Private key encryption failed: " + e.getMessage(), e);
   208	        }
   209	    }
   210	
   211	    public X509Certificate parseCertificate(String certPem) {
   212	        try (PEMParser parser = new PEMParser(new StringReader(certPem))) {
   213	            Object obj = parser.readObject();
   214	            if (obj instanceof X509CertificateHolder holder) {
   215	                return new JcaX509CertificateConverter()
   216	                    .setProvider(BouncyCastleProvider.PROVIDER_NAME)
   217	                    .getCertificate(holder);
   218	            }
   219	            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Invalid certificate PEM format");
   220	        } catch (Exception e) {
   221	            LOG.error("Failed to parse certificate", e);
   222	            throw new CertificateGenerationException("Certificate parsing failed: " + e.getMessage(), e);
   223	        }
   224	    }
   225	
   226	    public PrivateKey parsePrivateKey(String keyPem) {
   227	        try (PEMParser parser = new PEMParser(new StringReader(keyPem))) {
   228	            Object obj = parser.readObject();
   229	            JcaPEMKeyConverter converter = new JcaPEMKeyConverter()
   230	                .setProvider(BouncyCastleProvider.PROVIDER_NAME);
   231	
   232	            if (obj instanceof org.bouncycastle.openssl.PEMKeyPair pemKeyPair) {
   233	                return converter.getKeyPair(pemKeyPair).getPrivate();
   234	            } else if (obj instanceof org.bouncycastle.asn1.pkcs.PrivateKeyInfo pkInfo) {
   235	                return converter.getPrivateKey(pkInfo);
   236	            }
   237	            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Invalid private key PEM format");
   238	        } catch (Exception e) {
   239	            LOG.error("Failed to parse private key", e);
   240	            throw new CertificateGenerationException("Private key parsing failed: " + e.getMessage(), e);
   241	        }
   242	    }

   245	        try {
   246	            cert.checkValidity();
   247	        } catch (Exception e) {
   248	            throw new IllegalArgumentException("Certificate validation failed: " + e.getMessage(), e);
   249	        }

    34	 * @see <a href="https://docs.aws.amazon.com/acm/latest/APIReference/Welcome.html">AWS ACM API Reference</a>
    35	 */
    36	@ApplicationScoped
    37	public class AcmService {
    38	
    39	    private static final Logger LOG = Logger.getLogger(AcmService.class);
    40	    private static final int MAX_TAGS = 50;
    41	    private static final int MAX_TAG_KEY_LENGTH = 128;
    42	    private static final int MAX_TAG_VALUE_LENGTH = 256;
    43	    private static final int MAX_SANS = 100;
    44	    private static final int MAX_DOMAIN_LENGTH = 253;
    45	    private static final SecureRandom SECURE_RANDOM = new SecureRandom();
    46	
    47	    private final StorageBackend<String, Certificate> store;
    48	    private final CertificateGenerator certificateGenerator;
    49	    private final RegionResolver regionResolver;
    50	    private final int validationWaitSeconds;
    51	    private final AtomicInteger accountDaysBeforeExpiry = new AtomicInteger(45);
    52	    private final AtomicBoolean securityWarningLogged = new AtomicBoolean(false);
    53	
    54	    /**
    55	     * Idempotency token cache using lazy expiration (1-hour TTL).
    56	     *
    57	     * <p>Design decision: Using ConcurrentHashMap with timestamp-based entries
    58	     * instead of Caffeine or scheduled cleanup. This matches moto's approach
    59	     * (see moto/acm/models.py:478-505) where expired entries are removed on
    60	     * lookup. No background thread needed - acceptable for emulator workloads.</p>
    61	     *
    62	     * @see <a href="https://github.com/getmoto/moto/blob/main/moto/acm/models.py">moto ACM</a>
    63	     */
    64	    private final ConcurrentHashMap<String, IdempotencyTokenEntry> idempotencyTokenIndex = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
    65	
    66	    @Inject
    67	    public AcmService(StorageFactory factory, CertificateGenerator certificateGenerator,
    68	                      EmulatorConfig config, RegionResolver regionResolver) {
    69	        this(factory.create("acm", "acm-certificates.json",
    70	                new TypeReference<Map<String, Certificate>>() {}),
    71	            certificateGenerator,
    72	            regionResolver,
    73	            config.services().acm().validationWaitSeconds());
    74	    }
    75	
    76	    AcmService(StorageBackend<String, Certificate> store, CertificateGenerator certificateGenerator,
    77	               RegionResolver regionResolver, int validationWaitSeconds) {
    78	        this.store = store;
    79	        this.certificateGenerator = certificateGenerator;
    80	        this.regionResolver = regionResolver;
    81	        this.validationWaitSeconds = validationWaitSeconds;
    82	
    83	        // Validate Root CA resource availability
    84	        validateRootCaResource();
    85	    }
    86	
    87	    /**
    88	     * Log security warning once on first certificate creation/import.
    89	     * Uses AtomicBoolean to ensure thread-safe single logging.
    90	     */
    91	    private void logSecurityWarningOnce() {
    92	        if (securityWarningLogged.compareAndSet(false, true)) {
    93	            LOG.warn("SECURITY WARNING: ACM emulator stores private keys in plaintext. " +
    94	                     "This is acceptable for local development but NOT for production use.");
    95	        }
    96	    }
    97	
    98	    private void validateRootCaResource() {
    99	        try (InputStream is = getClass().getResourceAsStream("/certs/amazon-root-ca.pem")) {
   100	            if (is == null) {
   101	                LOG.warn("Amazon Root CA certificate not found at /certs/amazon-root-ca.pem - " +
   102	                         "certificate chains will be empty");
   103	            } else {
   104	                LOG.info("Amazon Root CA certificate loaded successfully");
   105	            }
   106	        } catch (IOException e) {
   107	            LOG.warnv("Failed to validate Root CA resource: {0}", e.getMessage());
   108	        }
   109	    }
   110	
   111	    // ============ RequestCertificate ============
   112	
   113	    public Certificate requestCertificate(String domainName, List<String> sans, ValidationMethod validationMethod,
   114	                                          String idempotencyToken, KeyAlgorithm keyAlgorithm,
   115	                                          String certAuthorityArn, CertificateOptions options,
   116	                                          Map<String, String> tags, String region) {
   117	        logSecurityWarningOnce();
   118	        validateDomainName(domainName);
   119	        validateSans(sans);
   120	        if (tags != null) {
   121	            validateTags(tags);
   122	        }
   123	
   124	        KeyAlgorithm alg = keyAlgorithm != null ? keyAlgorithm : KeyAlgorithm.RSA_2048;
   125	
   126	        // Check idempotency with parameter validation
   127	        if (idempotencyToken != null && !idempotencyToken.isEmpty()) {
   128	            int requestHash = computeRequestHash(domainName, sans, alg);
   129	            Optional<Certificate> existing = findByIdempotencyToken(idempotencyToken, region, requestHash);
   130	            if (existing.isPresent()) {
   131	                return existing.get();
   132	            }
   133	        }
   134	
   135	        String certId = UUID.randomUUID().toString();
   136	        String arn = buildCertificateArn(region, certId);
   137	
   138	        // Determine certificate type and initial status
   139	        CertificateType type;
   140	        CertificateStatus status;
   141	        if (certAuthorityArn != null && !certAuthorityArn.isEmpty()) {
   142	            type = CertificateType.PRIVATE;
   143	            status = CertificateStatus.ISSUED;
   144	        } else {
   145	            type = CertificateType.AMAZON_ISSUED;
   146	            status = validationWaitSeconds > 0 ? CertificateStatus.PENDING_VALIDATION : CertificateStatus.ISSUED;
   147	        }
   148	
   149	        // Generate real X.509 certificate
   150	        CertificateGenerator.GeneratedCertificate generated = certificateGenerator.generateCertificate(
   151	            domainName, sans, alg
   152	        );
   153	
   154	        Instant now = Instant.now();
   155	
   156	        Certificate cert = new Certificate();
   157	        cert.setArn(arn);
   158	        cert.setDomainName(domainName);
   159	
   160	        // Use LinkedHashSet for O(1) deduplication while preserving insertion order
   161	        LinkedHashSet<String> allSans = new LinkedHashSet<>();
   162	        allSans.add(domainName);
   163	        if (sans != null) {
   164	            allSans.addAll(sans);
   165	        }
   166	        cert.setSubjectAlternativeNames(new ArrayList<>(allSans));
   167	
   168	        cert.setStatus(status);
   169	        cert.setType(type);
   170	        cert.setValidationMethod(validationMethod != null ? validationMethod : ValidationMethod.DNS);
   171	        cert.setCreatedAt(now);
   172	        cert.setIssuedAt(status == CertificateStatus.ISSUED ? now : null);
   173	        cert.setNotBefore(generated.notBefore());
   174	        cert.setNotAfter(generated.notAfter());
   175	        cert.setSerial(generated.serial());
   176	        cert.setSubject(generated.subject());
   177	        cert.setIssuer(generated.issuer());
   178	        cert.setKeyAlgorithm(alg);
   179	        cert.setSignatureAlgorithm(generated.signatureAlgorithm());
   180	        cert.setCertificateBody(generated.certificatePem());

   210	
   211	    public Certificate describeCertificate(String certificateArn, String region) {
   212	        Certificate cert = getCertificateByArn(certificateArn, region);
   213	
   214	        // Check for expiration
   215	        if (cert.isExpired() && cert.getStatus() != CertificateStatus.EXPIRED) {
   216	            cert.setStatus(CertificateStatus.EXPIRED);
   217	            store.put(regionKey(region, cert.extractCertificateId()), cert);
   218	        }
   219	
   220	        return cert;
   221	    }

   224	
   225	    public Certificate getCertificate(String certificateArn, String region) {
   226	        return getCertificateByArn(certificateArn, region);
   227	    }

cat > /tmp/reproduce_acm_live.sh <<'EOF'
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
cd /testbed
PORT=${PORT:-18081}
LOG=/tmp/floci-acm-repro-server.log
rm -f "$LOG"
./mvnw -q -Dmaven.compiler.release=21 -Dquarkus.http.port=$PORT quarkus:dev >"$LOG" 2>&1 &
PID=$!
cleanup() { kill "$PID" >/dev/null 2>&1 || true; wait "$PID" >/dev/null 2>&1 || true; }
trap cleanup EXIT
for i in $(seq 1 90); do
  if grep -q "Listening on:.*:$PORT" "$LOG" || curl -fsS "http://localhost:$PORT/health" >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    break
  fi
  if ! kill -0 "$PID" >/dev/null 2>&1; then
    cat "$LOG"
    exit 1
  fi
  sleep 1
done
if ! kill -0 "$PID" >/dev/null 2>&1; then
  cat "$LOG"
  exit 1
fi
openssl req -x509 -newkey rsa:2048 -keyout /tmp/floci-key.pem -out /tmp/floci-cert.pem \
  -days 365 -nodes -subj "/CN=test.example.com" 2>/dev/null
CERT_B64=$(base64 -w0 /tmp/floci-cert.pem)
KEY_B64=$(base64 -w0 /tmp/floci-key.pem)
PASS_B64=$(printf 'test-passphrase' | base64 -w0)
ARN=$(curl -fsS -X POST "http://localhost:$PORT" \
  -H "X-Amz-Target: CertificateManager.ImportCertificate" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/x-amz-json-1.1" \
  -d "{\"Certificate\":\"$CERT_B64\",\"PrivateKey\":\"$KEY_B64\"}" \
  | sed -n 's/.*"CertificateArn"[[:space:]]*:[[:space:]]*"\([^"]*\)".*/\1/p')
test -n "$ARN"
EXPORT=$(curl -fsS -X POST "http://localhost:$PORT" \
  -H "X-Amz-Target: CertificateManager.ExportCertificate" \
  -H "Content-Type: application/x-amz-json-1.1" \
  -d "{\"CertificateArn\":\"$ARN\",\"Passphrase\":\"$PASS_B64\"}")
echo "$EXPORT" | grep -q -- "-----BEGIN CERTIFICATE-----"
echo "$EXPORT" | grep -q -- "-----BEGIN ENCRYPTED PRIVATE KEY-----"
echo "base64 blob import and imported cert export succeeded: $ARN"
EOF
chmod +x /tmp/reproduce_acm_live.sh
/tmp/reproduce_acm_live.sh

   169	    private String decodeBlob(String value) {
   170	        if (value == null || value.isEmpty()) {
   171	            return value;
   172	        }
   173	
   174	        // The ACM JSON 1.1 model defines certificate/key fields as blobs, so SDKs/CLI
   175	        // send them base64-encoded. Keep accepting the plain PEM strings that are
   176	        // convenient for hand-written requests and existing tests.
   177	        if (value.contains("-----BEGIN")) {
   178	            return value;
   179	        }
   180	
   181	        try {
   182	            return new String(Base64.getDecoder().decode(value), StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
   183	        } catch (IllegalArgumentException e) {
   184	            return value;
   185	        }
   186	    }

+    private String decodeBlob(String value) {
+        if (value == null || value.isEmpty()) {
+            return value;
+        }
+
+        // The ACM JSON 1.1 model defines certificate/key fields as blobs, so SDKs/CLI
+        // send them base64-encoded. Keep accepting the plain PEM strings that are
